Baddest fuckin song Iâ€™ve heard in along time.
This is a great song! It sounds new but also like something recorded around the Blood Sugar era with Frusciante's and Flea's seemingly intuitive string chemistry - that familiar trademark instrumental knit work meshed into the sound - and there is some seriously funky drumbeats melded with the plucked twangy bass lines that are satisfyingly vibrating my Wharfedale loudspeaker cabinets. A respectable dance groove to spin at any party and probably the nearest thing to anything they have done since 1991. Kiedis's lead vocals are brilliant here - and the backing vocals in the crescendo of the chorus are in a similar falsetto type vein (though a little more toned down) to backing vocals on Sir Psycho or If You Have to Ask. Overall it's a bit like a hypnotic time capsule - like a rediscovered gem from a Peppers previous recording session decades past that has only just resurfaced on a dusty old cassette tape rediscovered in Rick Rubin's house and that has been handed over to Flea who excitedly proceeds in blasting it out from his car stereo driving through the Hollywood Hills with a beaming smiled John sat next to him in the passenger seat, wind blowing through his long hair and ruffling his linen shirt.  ''Remember this one John!!??''  "Yeah.... wow, back in the day Flea!" Overall I love the bit with the enhanced spacey effects on the drumheads, the guitars and the elevating uplifting burst of the chorus. It's got all of the Chili Peppers magic in the mix.

How to Play the Game of Life Why do children wake up with their eyes wide open and jump out of bed while we open them just wide enough to see the phone so we can set it to snooze? Why are young people energetic and ready to â€œconquer the worldâ€ while older people are cautious and hesitant? Can we stay young-spirited forever? After all, if life is not a game, there is no excitement in it. And if there is no excitement in life, what is the point of living? If we want to keep enjoying, we need to make life a lifelong game. This game is very different from anything we know. It is not about what we can receive, but about what we can discover! By connecting to other people, we discover new worlds, other peopleâ€™s worlds! How do we achieve this? Quite simply, we need to focus on others rather than on ourselves. This may sound simple, but if you try it, you will realize how self-absorbed you are. We are all like that. Even those who feel that they are generous and giving are absorbed in their giving and do not see how much they do it for their own interest, and how they are focused on their own benefit when they give. Giving is fine, but the focus is the point here. Had the focus been on the receiver, the giver would have discovered countless revelations that are hidden from a self-centered eye. For the game to succeed, you need partners. It is impossible to play the game of giving without people to whom you can give and from whom you can receive. Therefore, there must be a group of people, up to ten or so, who play the game together. In order to succeed in discovering the other playersâ€™ worlds, we need to think good thoughts about them. Otherwise, we will have no incentive to approach them, no desire to discover their world. We can think good thoughts about each other if we do good things for one another. These can be the simplest things, but they must make us feel good about each other. Positive thoughts about each other bring us closer, and closeness opens our minds and hearts to others, so we can see the world through their eyes. As with any game, the more we practice, the better we get, and the harder, yet more rewarding the game becomes. But unlike any other game, as we improve in it, we will find that our entire perspective on life changes and expands, and we become wiser and more competent. The game of life, unlike any other game, reveals to us the secrets of life, the secrets of reality, because when you can look at something from all angles, nothing remains hidden from you.

I think a certainty about the Red Hot Chili Peppers is that every album, every song, and every sound that they have had over the years is on a consistent continuum of good vibes and high energy which can stir all kinds of moods in people when they listen.  Regardless of who is in the band, they just make great music and its good that they have experimented with various styles over the years but it was always clear that it was the same band creating soulful songs that speak to people and hit a nerve in a positive way. Alternating between funk, rock, pop, punk, rap, electronic etc. and also blending these genres of music together shows they want to evolve but also be distinctive which they are. I am glad they are still going strong, are popular, and let's all look forward to the new album.

This song is a masterpiece of art!
I saw Pearl Jam and Nirvana open for the Red Hots back in the 1990's. Yep. Really. But nothing has ever compared to the RHCP show I saw in a teensy club maybe 7 years prior, in the late 80's. The club had sound problems and they couldn't play for close to an hour. Crowd was getting impatient, drunk, and ugly. These were the days they performed in socks. Antony pulled out his left nut to entertain the crowd before they trashed the place. It worked and when the sound went back on they rocked the house with probably one of the most electrifying stage performances you could ever imagine. They played late to make up the delay and the crowd was so hyped up. It was utter madness. They've evolved so many times since those early days but their sound is always true to who they are. Love this. 90's revival in full force. If you like their music go see them live. I'm not sure you can experience the Red Hots fully until you see them perform in front of your own eyes. They're all incredible performers and Flea in his element is worth a whole other chapter. I bet they still rock it out. TBH it's probably better shows now he doesn't flash side junk as distraction. And in Antony's defense, he did obtain informed consent. I remember clearly he bellowed at the crowd, "I CAN'T MAKE IT GO ANY FASTER! WHAT DO YOU WANT ME TO DO, GIVE YOU MY LEFT NUT?!?!", and the crowd roared approval, so he obliged. Give em what they want, guys. Now & forever
